5a1(kha): ma rig 'khrul tshul ci ltar lags/ ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ nam mkha' gsal stong 'gyur med la/ sprin dang khu rlungs rje ba g.yos/ tsha grang / 
5a2(kha): 'khrug pa'i tsho 'dul byung / de bzhin rang 'byung g.yo mad sems/ nam mkha'i sangam rgya mtsho'i glong / dmigs med bdal bar gnas pa la/ sred bu bagnyal ma rig pa/ las 
5a3(kha): dang nyon mongs bag chags rkyen/ phyi rol log 'khrul shes pa'i yul/ rgyu rkyen las dang yul bzhi 'khrug/ 'bras bu khams gsum rgyu drug 'khor/ dper na re rab dmig 
5a4(kha): bzhin du/ mkha' la gzha' tshen sgra shad 'dzings/ nam mkha' bal 'dab lcags kbyu 'dzag/ ma rig log par 'khrul pa byung / yin men las la kun tu rtog/ bdag 
5a5(kha): 'dzin 'khrul pa blo yais bslud/ 'dzin pa rang rgyud du ma rtogs/ phyin ci log la shes pa rnyas/ gsum dang lnga dang drug dgu las/ brgyad khri bzhi stong skye 'phel rgyas/ dper na ras 
5a6(kha): la snum chen ltar/ dbral gyis mi khog dbyes mi phyed/ rgyu drug gnas su kha 'khor zhing / khams gsum 'khor ba'i rgya mtshor bying / srid pa gsum du 'pho 'djug byed/ phyin ci 
5b1(kha): log gi rgya mdud dam/ sdug bsngal 'khor ba'i tha dam bsdam/ bdag dang bdag gis 'dzin pa yis/ sna tshogs log 'khrul zhen pa spyod/ sdug bsngal tshad tshad 'dug tshul 
5b2(kha): gnas/ snang ba'i yul la chags pas bcings/ skye rga na 'chi'i chu bo bzhis/ chu gnyer rim bzhin zad du med/ bag chags sgrib pa sdug bsngal gnon/ mun pa bzhi' sgrib 
5b3(kha): rig pa 'gag/ 'khor ba'i las spyod grangs las 'das/ 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug dang / nga rgyal 'phrag dag khong khro ye/ shin tu rgyal ba'i gdug regs can/ bdud dang srin po 
5b4(kha): gnod sbyin bgegs/ sa bdag lha klu khyab 'jug tshogs/ dmu btsan 'tshams dang yi 'grogs bgegs/ sde brgyad lha srin gdug rtsub kyi/ cho 'phrul mi dge sna tshogs kun/ 
5b5(kha): rang gi mthu dang dpung du 'khrul/ phyin ci log tu rmongs pa'o// mkha' glong dbyings nas thugs rje skyes/ gdul bya'i dus la bab dus su/ gnyen po ye zhes snang ba 'char/ zhes 
5b6(kha): gsungs so// nyon mongs rang grol dug lnga rtsad gcod kyi rgyud las/ ma rig 'khrul tshul bstan pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// // 'khrul rtog 'joms pa'i gnyen po ni/ rang grol 
6a1(kha): 'dzin med con dbyings la/ rang 'byung y zhes thugs rje sha// dper na un nag shon me ltar/ log 'brul zhes pa'i rgyu rkyen las/ sul gyi gun par grol ba / 
6a2(kha): byas/ rgya che phyogs lung med par snyoms/ snying po ye shes 'od zer las/ rang 'byung ye shes che ba'i rgyan/ 'dzin pa rang grol dag pa la/ dri med ye shes snying po nyid/ dngos med 
6a3(kha): phyogs bral bon dbyings las/ skye ba med la s+dzu 'dhrul sku/ 'gag med nam mkhar nyi m shar/ phyi nang med par 'd po che/ mtshan ma'i rnam rtog zil gyis gnon/ gsum 
6a4(kha): dang lnga dang grangs med pa/ che ba'i yon tan mdzes pa'i rgyan/ sku gsum lhun grub dpe byad bzang / mtshan dpe yon tan zad med mdzod/ mkhyen pa'i ye shes rtogs pa'i phrul// 
6a5(kha): thabs kyi rgyal po 'gro 'dul sku/ log tog mtshan ma 'dzoms pa'i dpung / skye med dbyings la longs spyod rgyan/ spul sku grangs med bsam las 'das/ bsam gyis mi khyab 
6a6(kha): brjod mi long / zhi rgyas dbang drag mngon spyod du / rigs dang sde tshan zhing khams bcas/ so sor spul zhing gnyen por shar/ smra bsam brjod dang bral ba la/ thugs kyi klong brdol / 
6b1(kha): parhu'i lces/ brgyad khri bzhi stong bon gyi sgo/ brgyud lung man ngag bsam las 'das/ drang don nges don ston pa'i bka'/ rang gsal theg pa rgyu'i bon/ bka' yi bye brag phun sum / 
6b2(kha): tshogs/ gang ltar dad mos gnyen po shar/ rang 'byung ye shes thams cad mkhyen/ rnam rtog mi mnga'dran rig thugs/ rgyu rkyen med pa'i snying po nyid/ ma bcos kun gzhi byang chub / 
6b3(kha): sems/ stong zhing bdag med con gyi dbyings/ phyi nang kun gsal rtog pa med/ phyogs ris med pa mnyam pa'i ngang / phyi dang rang rig mtshan nyid 'dzin/ bya brtsal med pa grub pa'i 
6b4(kha): las/ rang bzhin 'od gsal rnam par dag/ ye shes 'od zer gsal ba'i mdangs/ ma sgrib ye shes mkhyen pa'i mdzod/ dbang dang byin rlabs dngos grub gter/ mi rtogs 'gro 'dul 
6b5(kha): thabs la mkhas/ ma rig dug 'dzoms gnyen por shar/ rang 'byung yon tan phun sum tshogs/ yid bzhin nor bu 'phrul po che/ ye shes 'odi zer che ba'i rgyan/ gser gyi nye 
6b6(kha): ma rang 'byung sku/ 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i stobs po che/ lhun grub yon tan rang dag gsal/ legs pa kun 'byung thugs rjer grub/ nam mkha'i dbyings dang rgya mtsho'i klong / thub 
7a1(kha): pa med pa'i snying por gsal/ csho' yangs 'o yon tan mchog/ kun snyoms yon tan snying po n// khyab badal lhun grub ye shes cheo/ mdzad pa rnam dag un sum 
7a2(kha): tshogs/ bya bral rtsol sgrub bral ba'i sding / 'phren las mthar bhyin lhun gyis grub/ mdzad spyed thabs kyi ye zhes kyi/ zhan chags med pa'i dbyings su pbyor/ kun grub 'phrin / 
7a3(kha): las gnyen po shar/ nyon mongs rang grol dug lnga rtsad gcod kyi rgyud las/ gnyen po ye shes kyi gnas lugs bstan pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// / dus gsum 'gyur med g.sung 
7a4(kha): dung sems/ bskal par mi nub rgyal mtshan can/ srid par 'khyams kyang sems mi stor/ 'byung ba 'khrug kyang yid mi bsgribs/ dus gsum bral kyang dbyings mi nyams/ stong 
7a5(kha): gsum 'gyur kyang klong mi 'gag/ khams gsum 'thib kyang mkha' mi bsgribs/ rang gsal rang stong 'gyur ba med/ skad cig gcig la s+dzogs mnyam nyid/ rang gsal dang 'byung 
7a6(kha): ye shes nyid/ stong pa bon nyid dbyings su grol/ de gsum mi phyed gcig gi ngang / mnyam nyid phyogs riMs med par gnas/ brtsal du med pa'i ye shes che/ 'du 'bral med pa lhun / 
7b1(kha): grub gnas/ rtag chad mta' bral chen por dag/ dag pa nyid kyang dag la 'das/ 'das pa'i bon la bshad du med/ dper na nam mkha'i og dbyings ltar/ mi mthun gang dang mthun / 
7b2(kha): pa la/ yin ni cer yang ma yin par/ 'char ni cer yang 'char ba la/ grub ni mtshan mar ma grub pa/ mtha' mar ltung ba'i ye zhes nyid/ 'phel 'greb med pa'i ngo bor gnas// 
7b3(kha): lta ba'i don gnas rangs zin/ nyon mongs rang grol chen po yais/ dug lnga rang gi rtsa ba chod/ rnam tog chu bran rka chad 'dra/ 'khor ba'i zhings dbyings su thim/ srid pa mi nub 
7b4(kha): g.sung dung sems/ phyogs su ma lung lta ba'i gnas/ gzhi rtsa med pa'i snying po la/ gzugs su ma grub mtshan ma med/ phung po byang sems mngon par shes/ smra bsam brjod dang 
7b5(kha): bral ba la/ dran rig mi 'khrul g.yung drung thugs/ che ba'i yon tan sprul pa'i rgyan/ rtsol sgrub med par spyod las 'das/ rang 'byung rig pa spyi byugs shar/ bon sku'i rtsa ba / 
7b6(kha): byang chub sems/ sems la ma gtogs bon rnams med/ sems nyid rtogs pa'i khyad par la/ che ba'i yon tan rtsal ma 'gag/ mya ngan 'das pa'i bon du shar/ sems nyid ma 
8a1(kha): rtogs 'khrul pa las/ log shes tshe 'prul bsam mi khyag/ 'khor ba'i tson rnams na tshigs nar/ sems nyid gsas mkhar ci ltar na/ ga bzhi'i gnsdu ma 
8a2(kha): grub la/ mu bzhi' gong du ma 'gag pa'o// sems nyid gsas mkhar yod pa mina/ yod na stong du ga la 'dod/ rnam par rtog pa 'gag pa med/ mya ngan 'da' ba gang zhig 'ong / 
8a3(kha): gzheg pa'i dngos po grol mi 'gyur/ sems nyid gsas mkhar med pa min/ med na rig pa ci ltar 'char/ rnam pa thams cad ci ltar mkhyen/ 'khor ba rgyu drug lung mi srid/ 
8a4(kha): thar pa'i 'bras bu lam mi rnyed/ sems nyid gsas mkhar gnyis ka min/ yin na gnyis su 'drer 'dres / mi rung / rnam rtog mi mnga' cir yang gsal/ gsal la mi rtog 
8a5(kha): 'byung mi 'gyur/ sems nyid gsas mkhar gnyis med min/ yin na rtogs dang ma rtogs dang / 'khor ba mya ngan 'das pa dang / gnyen po nyon mongs 'byung mi 'gyur/ rang bzhin 
8a6(kha): / lhun grub snying po nyid/ mkha' klong dbyings kyi gsas mkhar du / ci yang ma yin cir yang 'char/ ma grub ma 'gag gcig la s+dzogs/ zhen pa'i sgros 'dog skur 'debs med// 
8b1(kha): kun grol gsas mkhar chen po ste/ nub pa med pa'i rgyal mtshan can/ dper na nam mkha' khyung chen bzhin/ spyi rgya rlabs kyis chod par gnas/ mkha' la nyi ma shar ba 
8b2(kha): ltar/ kun la gsal zhing snyoms par gnas/ rgya mtsho chen po'i klong yangs ltar/ phyi nang snod bcud s+dzogs par gnas/ nyon mongs rang grol dug lnga rtsad gcod kyi rgyud las/ lha / 
8b3(kha): ba rang grol bstan pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// // g.yung drung ye khebs gsas mkhar lta ba la/ gar yang mi btsal spyod pa kun las 'das/ dmigs med mi g.yo rang sems ye thub / 
8b4(kha): tu/ dbyings nas mi nyams klong nas mi g.yo zhing / mkha' la mi 'khrugs cig le cig tu bzhag/ rig pa stong gsal 'gyur med dbyings nyid du / lus kyi bya byed ci bder bcos 
8b5(kha): pa dang / byeng rgod dbugs nyid cha la dbab pa dang / yid kyi blon pos bya ra stong byas nas/ shes pa phyi'i yul dang rig pa nang gi sems/ nam mkha'i rang bzhin khyab bdal chen po ru/ 
8b6(kha): mi yengs lhang ng lhan nar dgongs pa gsal/ rig pa lhangs kyi gsal ba'i lhag mthong la/ rig pa nges bzung bral ba'i zhi gnas mchog/ stong gsal dbyer med zung du 'brel ba'i / 
9a1(kha): con/ ma yings pa la gnas pa rtogs pa'i phrul/ nga dang rang bzhin ma bcos bdag nyid par/ 'gyur med sprois dang bral ba'i dbyings su bnag/ me g.si dbyings la kun 
9a2(kha): 'byung krong 'khug ste/ mkha' la log par snang ba'i rzes 'breng nas/ rtog pas nang bkang spyod pas bhye bkang zhing / 'dzin pas bdag bcing gzung bas gzhan bcing nas/ gsas 
9a3(kha): mkhar g.sung drung sems kyi don mi gsal/ rtsol bas bya brtsal 'khrul pa'i dmag gsab tu/ dmyal ba'i grong bzung ngan song btsen du khrid/ thar pa'i lam bral byang chub sems 
9a4(kha): dang 'gyangs / khams gsum 'khor ba'i gnas las grol mi 'gyur/ khams gsum 'khor ba gting nas sugs pa'i phyir/ g.yung drung ye khyab gsas mkhar snying po ru/ gar spyin / 
9a5(kha): rtsi la snang shrong / ma chags pa bzhin/ dbyings dang rig pa gnyis med gang la gnas/ ma yengs mi 'gyur don gsal lhun grub gnas/ 'bras bu brtsal med rnam pa thams cad 
9a6(kha): mkhyen/ rtog med rang grol chen po'i dbyings su 'gyur/ nyon mongs rang grol dug lnga rtsad gcod kyi rgyud las/ dgongs pa rang grol bstan pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// // lha dgongs 
9b1(kha): gnyis med 'du 'bral med pa ru/ snang ba rang grol rang shar spyod pa'i mchog/ lus mi nub dang 'dus ma byas pa'i sku/ ngag mi nub pa sgra dang bral ba'i gsung / yid mi nub pa bsam / 
9b2(kha): las 'das pa'i thugs/ mkha' kglong dbyings su bdal pa chen po'i gsas/ spyod pa'i dgongs pa mdzad pa thugs rje che/ ma lus ma pbye blang dor med snyoms par/ che chung bzang ngan 
9b3(kha): med par kun gsal dag/ gzung 'dzin 'khrul ba'i bon du snang b kun/ rang bzhin 'jzig dang 'gag pa med par 'gyur/ brtag tu mi bzod 'khor ba'i bon/ phyi ye 'jig rten 
9b4(kha): snod 'di dag/ rang bzhin 'jig chags stong gnas grol/ dbyar rgun sten dbyed dus bzhir 'gyur/ bzung yang mi zin dgags mi khegs/ rang bzhin 'byung zhing rang bzhin grol/ 
9b5(kha): skye rga na 'chi 'pho 'gyur zhing / sdug bsngal las dang bya byed kyi/ mi gnas 'gyur bzhin tu che/ bzung bas mi zen dgags mi khegs/ rang bzhin 'byung zhing rang bzhin grol/ 
9b6(kha): sems kyi 'gyur ldog yid kyi bon/ skad cig mi gnas dus gsum 'gyur/ bzung bas mi zin dgags mi khegs/ rang bzhin byung zhing rang bzhin grol/ rang grol chen po spyod / 
10a1(kha): pa'i mchog/ bde skyed longs spyed pun sdum tshigs/ byams sdug gnyen mtshan thams cad la/ nhen med rang kgrol khyod pa'i mtcshog/ dug cing 'pengs pa mi 
10a2(kha): khams yul/ dgra sdang rgol ba thams cad la/ sdang med rang grol spyod pa'i prul/ bye dang nang gi bsdus pa'i bon/ sems dang sems las byung ba rnams/ rang 'byung ye zhes dag pa 
10a3(kha): las/ rang grol gzug ma'i spyod pa yi/ yengs med s thub lhun la bhags/ dper na 'dam gyi pad mo lthar/ nyes pa'i skyen bral yon tan s+dzogs/ gsas mkhar sgo gsum 
10a4(kha): spyod pa 'di/ mzhen ma chags lhug par thing / thugs rje thabs kyi sprul pa yi/ 'gro ba log 'khrul don ma bzung / yi shes sprul pa'i kpyod pa yis/ dgongs pa'i don gsal 
10a5(kha): nyams su blangs/ byin rlabs nus pa spyod pa yis/ tdhug cing dregs pa'i log tog gzhom/ mthun 'jug thabs kyi spyod pa zad/ spyod pa bon nyid ma bcos pa/ dper na sang ge / 
10a6(kha): rtsal s+dzogs bzhin/ nyam ng med par grol bar 'gyur/ nyon mongs rang grol drug lnga rtsad gcod kyi rgyud las/ spyod pa rang grol du bstan pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// / 'bras bu / 
10b1(kha): brtsal med sangs rgyas dngs/ thub pa med pa'i rgyal mtshan can/ 'gyur ba med pa gsung drung sku/ 'du 'bral med pa byang chub sems/ thig mtha' med pa'i ye shes can/ rang / 
10b2(kha): 'byung yo shes snying po nyied/ rangs zen na 'bras ba mchog/ bya brtsal rtsol sgrub bral ba'i gng / mi tog yo zhes dgongs pa'i thugs/ gsal steng 'gyur med lhan gyis grub/ 
10b3(kha): mkha' gsal rangs zin pa yin/ rnam pa thams cad cir yang mkhyen/ ma rig rmongs pa'i 'khrul ba sangs/ thugs rje ye shes dpag med shar/ mya ngan 'das pa'i mthar mi ltung / 
10b4(kha): klong stong rangs zin pa'i/ ng dang bdag tu 'dzin pa grol/ dmigs pa'i mtha' rnams kun dang bral/ mi rtog ye shes rang 'byung shar/ bdal pa chen po kun la khyab/ 'khor ba'i 
10b5(kha): mtha' las 'das par gnas/ 'gyur med dbyings mnyams zin la/ skye rga na 'chi bzhi dang bral/ dus gsum 'gyur ba'i klong las grol/ me thub gsung dung rgyal mtshan can/ 
10b6(kha): 'bras bu bla med sangs rgyas teng / 'das pa'i bde bar gshegs pa yang / rang rigs zin mngon sangs rgyas/ da lta bzhugs pa'i bon gnhan kyang / rang rig sgom pa'i 'bras bu thob/ 
11a1(kha): sla nas 'byen pa'i lha gzhen kyang / rang rig rtogs pa'i 'bras ba yin/ 'bras ba gzhan na re ba med/ rang gsal rtogs pas tsams cad mkhyen/ rang nying rtogs / 
11a2(kha): pas bdag 'dzin 'gags/ gnyis med rtogs pas mya ngan 'das/ yang dag lhun grub 'bras bu than/ nyon mongs rang grol drug lnga rtsad gcod kyi rgyud las/ 'bras bu rang grol du 
11a3(kha): bstan pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// // bon nyid mi 'gyur spros bral dkyil 'khor nas/ rang 'byung ye shes 'gyur med 'di ru gsal/ mi gsal gsal ba'i bdag nyid can/ bdag 
11a4(kha): phyogs bral ba'i byang chub sku/ chen gang 'od kyis kun tu khyab/ rang bzhin mnyam nyid bon sku las/ rgyan dang cha lugs mtshan dpe longs spyod s+dzogs/ mnyam la ma 'dres 
11a5(kha): sprul pa'i sku/ ngo bo yid bzhin nor bu nyid/ sku lnga mthar bhyin bder gshegs lnga/ gnhen lha rig pa'i snying po nyid/ ma pa thugs nyid dbyings chen te/ khri khug dngos med nam 
11a6(kha): bba' gyusr bntanbala bya/ bba glas n mye rnam pa g/ an 'dzin bya ba san bhins// bhyeng kyi b 'byalthag par la/ bya lng 'dzan / 
11b1(kha): pa'i zhen pa grol/ klong nas sprul pa lha'i gsas/ gsas rje kun 'byung chen po'i klong / rgod gsas thugs rje tshad med klong / gnam sras kun spul chen po'i kling / gar gsas 
11b2(kha): mngon spul chen po'i glong / ghen rab mtshan med dag pa'i gling / klong gi tsho 'dul rigs lnga lhar/ regs lngar 'dzin pa'i rtog pa grol/ ba ga klong chen syangs pa nas/ 'byung 
11b3(kha): ba rnam lnga'i sprul pa shar/ mtshan med dag pa'i gnas 'gyur bas/ mkha' lnga sprul pa'i yum chen rnams/ byin rlabs bag ldan klong du shar/ yum du 'dzin pa'i chags pa 
11b4(kha): grol/ cir gsal mkha' la sprul pa'i rtsal/ yi gnhen ye sman 'dus pa'i lha/ cer snang ye shes nyid las byung / yod par 'dzin pa'i chags pa grol/ brtson 'grus mthar / 
11b5(kha): phyin sprul pa'i rtsal/ dus gsum ston pa gtsug pud can/ sgo ba yab yum la sogs te/ phyag rgya dkyil 'khor zhi ba'i lha/ rang la byung zhing rang la grol/ 'phrul chen zhi / 
11b6(kha): ba'i lha tshogs dang / mkha' klong dbyings kyi cho 'dul yin/ snang la dngos med gzha' tchen lta bu'i tshul/ sku mdog phyag mtshan me long 'di bzhin gsal/ rgyan dang cha lugs 
12a1(kha): glu bla'i dkyil 'khor s+dzogs/ skye ba med la skye ba'i tsho 'brul du/ log tog 'gro 'dul sku ru bstan pa yang / 'dzin pa'i yul med gzung ba'i thabs las grol/ 
12a2(kha): s+dzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mkhyen pa'i ye shes dang / mdzad pa'i 'phrin las gsum du sprul pa yang / s+dzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bder gshegs rigs lnga nyid/ thugs rje byin rlabs rgyu / 
12a3(kha): lnga'i sems can la/ ji ltar 'tshams pa bzhin du 'gro don mdzad/ mkhyen pa'i ye shes dri med ye shes lnga/ byin rlabs thabs kyi ye shes sna tshogs pa/ 'dul ba'i thugs dza / 
12a4(kha): bye brag bsam mi khyab/ mdzad pa'i 'phrin las grol ba'i lam chen lngas/ thugs rje byin rlabs 'gro don s+dzogs par mdzad/ rang 'byung bon gsum thabs kyi khyad par ni/ ye / 
12a5(kha): shes sgyu mar snang zhing gong ma yi/ ma yang kun spyod ci la mi gnas shing / don dam rgya mtsho nam mkha'i ngag lhar dag/ ting 'dzin bye brag thabs kyi cho 'drul las/ 'byung ba 
12a6(kha): rim brtsegs dkyil 'khor ci snang ba/ ye shes mkha' yangs ba ga'i klong du grol/ gzhal yas yid bzhin lhun gyis grub pa yang / skyon med yon tan phun sum tshogs ldan 
12b1(kha): pa/ che ba'i yon tan rnam dag mkha' la grol/ 'od zer sna tshogs phyogs bcur 'phro ba yang / stong gsum 'jig rten khengs pa'i thugs rje ldan/ thugs rje chen pos phyogs 
12b2(kha): med yongs su grol/ rin chen khri rkang phyogs bzhir gsal ba yang / bder gshegs dkyil 'khor 'degs pa'i mthu ldan zhing / bdud bzhi 'dul ba'i phyag rgya chen por grol/ 
12b3(kha): sang ge glang chen a dang ba bya dang / hang shang ma hte lasogs khri rnams kyang / mi 'jigs stobs mchog +dzu 'dul rkang pa dbang / thar pa mya ngan 'das pa grol ba'i lam/ che ba'i / 
12b4(kha): yon tan gzhan las dpag pa'i phyir/ theg pa'i nang nas rgyal po lta bu ste/ thabs kyi 'dul ba'i phyag rgya chen por grol/ pa rma mdzes sdug 'od du 'bar ba yang / nyes pa'i skyon 
12b5(kha): bral yon tan phun sum tshogs/ sna tshogs 'byung bas skye ba bzhi sgo kheg/ rnam dag yon tan chen po'i phyag rgya grol/ rin chen nyi zla 'od du snang ba dang / 'jig rten yongs 
12b6(kha): su sgron mer snang ba dang / stong gsum mun nag sel ba'i mthu ldan pa/ yab yum gnyis med byang chub sems su grol/ 'gyur med g.yung drung phyag rgyas skur gsal ba/ 'gro 
13a1(kha): / 'al kbyil 'tshor bal kyi ho khyab/ bde gzhegs rnam kyi tlogs rji' dan' gon to/ gcog pa 'did glur bgyur gi thlog sdobo/ phyogs md ni / 
13a2(kha): thams thabs kyi bhyag rgyar grol/ rgyan dang cha lugs mzes pa na tshogs kun/ yon tan rgyan gyis gdul bya r re 'dzoms/ dngos su ma grub glua tla' dkyil 'khor bzhin/ 
13a3(kha): tsho 'drul thabs kyi phyag rgya chen por grol/ 'phan dang zar tshags dang rgyal mtshan dang / bla r gdugs lasogs pa bsam mi khyab/ con gyi ru mtshon dbyings su pbyar lasogs/ 
13a4(kha): bdu bzhi mgo bsnal ngan sing gting bzhan nas/ gdul bya'i gnyen po gzhan las khyad par 'phags/ pa rol zal gyis gnon pa'i batha ldan pa/ bon nyid klong nas rol pa

5a4(tha'o): dngas ma/ srid pa'i thog ma/ 'byung ba'i snying po la/ yul 'di ma mdzes pa'i tshal zhes bya ba ru/ yab rgyal po gsal 'di 'bar zhes bya ba dang / yum legs pa'i rgyal sgron ma 
5a5(tha'o): zhes bya ba gnyis la/ sras lham dral ni mi mnga' ste/ shin tu longs spyod dang ldan zhing bde skyed phun sum 'tshogs par gnas so// de la 'khor dang g.yog dang bran po bran mo las / 
5a6(tha'o): sogs pa mang pos bskor zhing mnga'dar bar gnas so// de'i tshe de'i dus na/ bran gyi nang nas dman rigs da gon zhes bya ba gcig dang / yum legs pa'i rgyal sgron ma bya ba 
5b1(tha'o): gnyis 'thab cing rtsod par 'gyur to// de yab kyi dgongs pas bran gyis ldog par mi rigs dgongs nas/ yum gyi kha 'dzin du dmigs te/ thags kyi thu lum brim te btang bas/ 
5b2(tha'o): bran la sog te zhi bar gyur to// de yi tshe yab yum de gnyis zhin tu skyengs shing 'gyod pa drag po'i sems skyes nas/ rab tu yi mug mi dga' ste/ dad pa'i rlan la snying rje'i ser / 
5b3(tha'o): bslang / dge ba'i stobs bskyed do// phyogs bcu kun du skor ba dang lha phyag bya'o// me tog gtor zhing sgre ngag bstan no// dge ba phun sum tshogs par bskyed do// sbyin pa dmigs pa / 
5b4(tha'o): med par btang / rin po che sna tshogs kyi mchod pa sul/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo brgya rtsa brgyad bskor/ bka' yi 'khor lo chen po yongs su bskor/ smin lam grangs med pa mang 
5b5(tha'o): po btab go/ yab yum zhin tu gdung ba'i sgre ngag ni/ su yi snyan du bon cing gsan na/ 'od zer 'du 'phro'i gnas su dbyings kyi lha mkha' 'gying kha yi snyan du gsan no// lha 
5b6(tha'o): yis thugs rje gnhen la bskul te/ ston pa gnhen rab kyis/ mthing gur g.yu 'thib kyi gsas mkhar du / 'gro ba thugs rjes bzung ba'i dgongs pa mdzad do// de nas cung zhig 
6a1(tha'o): // tsam na/ rgyal po yab yum de gnyis tshe 'phos nas/ dge ba'i stobs smon lam gyi ba thus/ sum zhu rtsa gsum lha yi gnas/ srid yul lha mdangs zhes bya ba ra/ 
6a2(tha'o): bya ye sred cing sprul pa'i sras/ yab yang rgyal lha yi rgyal po zhes bya ba cig sku 'khrungs te/ shin tu mnga'dar zhing bsod nams che ba/ nyin zhig ni khye'u chung gsu'i zur pud 
6a3(tha'o): can brgya yis bskor nas/ blu gar dang rol mo 'brul lo// mtshan zhig na rin po che'i mun la 'bar/ gss 'od kyi gdan la bzhugs te/ lha yi bu m ren po che'i ze' 
6a4(tha'o): phrog can brgya yis bskor nas/ me tog mdangs kyi mchod pa 'brul ba bzhin du bsod nams che zhing / mnga' dar bar gnas pa la/ khab dang dbyal du ma mchis te/ phyogs bcu / 
6a5(tha'o): kun tu rmad btang ba la/ yul srin yul stag tshal zhes bya na/ sa bdag stag gdong lde rgyal gyi sras mo/ yum stag za he ting gi rgyal mo bya ba zhig 'khrungs te/ shin tu 
6a6(tha'o): mtshan bzang zhing gzi brjid che ba/ yid du 'ong zhing ng tshul bzang ba/ spyi bo'i gtsug na rin po che'i 'di 'phro ba de/ khab dang dbyal du bzhes so// de nas dus zhig na/ stag zag
6b1(tha'o): he ting shin tu sku nyams dma' ba cig gi rmaM lam la/ lhags kyi ma la khri chu'i gdong pa can/ zla ches gtam pa'i mchi ba can/ yan lag zangs kyi sara khyim du 'dug pa/ 
6b2(tha'o): lag na snying chen rlin pa tsogs pa zhig dang brtse zhing rol pa rnaMs/ 'di nag po mda' tsam zhig kyang rnam du zhugs pa rmaMs/ nangs par rnal sang nam langs tsam na/ snying yang mi 
6b3(tha'o): dga' pyod pyod yaengs yengs byed/ mngal yang rtsub la rnam yang laM/ shin tu 'jzigs shing ba spu'i bu g kun kyang zing zing por gyur/ khab nas con te lha yul 'di ma'i tshal/ 
6b4(tha'o): mdzes pa'i me tog gling la zhabs 'chags su byen pas/ shar phyogs nas snga zhig dang dang zer bsnyams byed/ shar du gzigs pas/ lhoa ru nga zhig dang dang zer bsnyams byed/ lho na 
6b5(tha'o): gzigs na bub nassnga sgra cig dang dang zer basnyams byed/ thub tu gzigs tsam na/ byang phyogs nas sgra cig dang dang zer bsnyams byed/ byang na gzigs pas/ steng phyogs nasnga 
6b6(tha'o): sgra cig dang dang zer ba snyams byed/ steng du gzigs pas 'og nasnga sgra cig dang dang zer ba snyams byed/ 'og tu gzigs pas steng 'og spyi bo'i thad ka nas snga sgra cig daing dang zer ba 
7a1(tha'o): / snyams byed de/ phyogs mtshams kun tu gzigs pas dngos po'i gzugs su ma grub par/ snyan pa'i sgra spyi bo'i gtsug na grags nas/ lha dang gss kyi sprul pa 
7a2(tha'o): cig yin nam thugs la dgongs nas/ mngala yang rtsub la rnam yang laM/ rab tu bsdungs par gnas kyang sems gzings bstod do// mtshod s+dzas longs spyod sna tshogs bshams te/ 
7a3(tha'o): bar phyogs su mar me'i mchod pa pbul/ lho phyogs snga gshang sgra yi mchod pa pul/ thub phyogs su dri zham songs kyi mchod pa sul/ byang phyogs su gtsang ma khus kyi mchod pa 
7a4(tha'o): pdul/ lho shar du lha s+dzas kyi mchod pa sul/ lho bub na me tog gi mchod pa pul/ byang thub na ren po che'i mchod pa bul/ byang shar na longs spyod kyi mchod pa pul/ steng 
7a5(tha'o): phyogs su rgyan ldan lhab hub kyi mchod pa sbul/ dbus su mnyam nyid phyag rgya'i mchod pa sul/ gser gyi ldeng bu phyag tu pud nas/ phyogs bcu kun tu bdar zhing mchod pa / 
7a6(tha'o): phrul/ g.yu yi ldem mdngas mgul nas bkrol te/ phyogs bcu kun du bdal zhing mchod pa phrul/ nas dkar mo 'bru bdun gang rtsa g.yas nas gtor te/ nam mkha'i dbyings 
7b1(tha'o): su gtor nas smod du 'dzug/ phyogs bcu kun tu lha phyag 'tshal zhing skyabs 'gro byas/ gdung ba'i sgre ngag bton te/ stag za hi ting rgyal mo yis/ za 'og pad ma res kyi gdan 
7b2(tha'o): bteng / darg dkar gsung du srhaMs kyi sngas byas/ be d ren po che'i 'd dang / mtshong mdog pad ma raMs kyi sku rten g.yas g.yon byas/ nye zla 'khor lo res la rgyab gtad d/ kha thub tu 
7b3(tha'o): gzigs nas bzhugs pas/ cung zhig na phyogs bcu nas sgra snyan yid du 'ong ba mang po grags so// de nas cung zhig na/ shin tu mdzes pa'i skyes mchog khyad par can/ sku la 
7b4(tha'o): stag gi lcags pa'i ral ga la/ me lce 'phro ba'i rgyan bkye ba/ rin po che sna tshogs kyis spras pa ni gsol/ mgul la rin po che'i shel gyi car lang ni btags/ dbu gtsug 
7b5(tha'o): na rin po che 'di 'bar bstag gi srog zhu me lce bskyil ba'i chod paT dbu la bnab/ phyag na gser gyisnga chung dang dang brung ba cig/ stag za' mdun du yer gyi byin nas/ stag 
7b6(tha'o): za he ting kag gis bzhengs/ rab tu yid spro sems dad nas/ dga' ba'i mdngs pbyungs gus phyag 'tshal/ brtse gdung ngag gis 'di skad brjod/ shin tu rgyan bzang skyes mchog khyad / 
8a1(tha'o): / @/ par can/ sprul pa'i stobs ldan gzi brjid dbang gi sku/ nad kyis gdung ba'i sdug bsngal ma lus sel/ yid 'ong mdzes pa khyed la phyag 'tshal lo// bdag ni ston / 
8a2(tha'o): mongs gner gyur za ma mo'i lus/ mdong gsum rmaM lam ma bzang nas/ da nang lus kyi bro 'tshal te/ khyim du 'dug snying ma tshar nas/ 'odi ma mzhes tshal gling du mchis/ 
8a3(tha'o): nyams la phyogs bni steng 'og nas/ rasgra dang dang gsung byungs nas/ dad pa'i stobs kyi gzings bstod d// phyogs mtshams steng 'og bla bzu ru/ mchod pa'i yo byad longs spyod sul// 
8a4(tha'o): lha phyag 'tshal zhing me tog pul/ smre ngag bton nas smon lam btab/ za 'og gdan la sar mchis pas/ phyogs bcu kun nas sgra snyan grags/ da lta skyes mchog nyid dang 
8a5(tha'o): mdal/ lus kyang yang zhing snyoms par snyams/ bri 'tshams 'di yang sud tsam bad/ skyes mchog dam pa lha yi gnhen/ 'od zer slob dpon gnyen lags sam/ gang lags 
8a6(tha'o): bka' gsal lung bstan 'tshal/ zhes zhus pas/ skyes bu chen po'i bka' stsal pa// gani lha yi sprul pa yin/ stag za h ting rgyal mo yi/ sngon cho skye ba snga ma la/ dge 
8b1(tha'o): sdig 'tshol bar spyod pa de/ bud med rang bzhin rgyud ngan las/ bran dang 'thab nas yab la bskul/ yab kyi lhags kyi tbhu lum gyis/ bran phrug ma mie d gon bsad/ bran phug / 
8b2(tha'o): zhe sdang gdug sems dang / sngon las rnam smin dbang btsan nas/ da lta dus cig gnas cig tu/ bdud kyi las dbang rab btsan zhing / srin gyi bar chad mthu che bas/ srin po mar 
8b3(tha'o): mer lang tshe la/ srin gyi cho 'phrul yum la 'byung / lthcags gyi mi la zangs gyi thar khyim can/ khro chu'i 'dzer gdong bya ba yin/ de la rtse rol 'dod pas spyod nas kyang / 'od 
8b4(tha'o): nag mda' tsam lhums su zhugs pa ni/ srin po'i bur spul sngon gyi bran bhug yin/ na tsha rnam lce mi bde ba ni/ sngon gyi lan chags dad pa yin/ yum la srin gyi cho / 
8b5(tha'o): 'drul zhugs pa de/ dbyings kyi lha lngas thugs rje' spyan gyis gzigs/ srin gyi rang bzhin sdug la skyon che bas/ rnam nas 'dul ba'i gnyen po cig/ lha yi yul nas ma 
8b6(tha'o): btang na/ shul nas btul bas mi thul te/ rnam du zhugs na ma la za/ de nas sems can yongs la gnod/ rnam nas 'dul ba'i gnyen po zhig/ spun zla'i tshul du da rung 'ong / 
9a1(tha'o): / dkbyis 'jug pa'i pul bate/ sngon gyi dge stobs thon lam bblang / gsung du lha yi sul bcig/ mkha' 'byi thugs las sul pa'i sras/ log la 'dul / 
9a2(tha'o): ba'i dragzhul can/ srin po 'dul ba'i stobs chen cig/ de nub rnam du zhugs par mchis/ nga ni gnhen rab mi bo ste/ lha yi ston pas nga mngag nas/ khyod la lung bstan 'ong 
9a3(tha'o): ba yin/ stag za he tang rgyal mo khyod/ de bub dgon oggs bon// styid dad skyes la/ gzim khar rmig lam smon lam thob/ de nub rmaM lam ci byung pa/ song gdus su nga 'ong gi/ 
9a4(tha'o): nangs par nga la ston du shog/ zhes lung bstan te/ ston pa gshen rab mi bo nyid/ bon yul 'di ma tshal gling na/ mthing gur g.su 'thib gsas khang du / dgongs pa la gshegs te/ 
9a5(tha'o): sum la thugs kyi dang gong nas/ yid kyi cho 'prul la sprul pa'i 'od zer bkyi'o// yum stag za he tang gis/ thub mi mchod pa'i longs spyod rgya chen bshams/ mos pa'i / 
9a6(tha'o): sems bskyed/ spro ba'i tshig gis mtchod pa rgya cher pul zhing / smon lam btab ste gzim pa'i rmaM lam la/ stag 'jam rgod pa'i sku lus la/ glog dmar gyes pa'i thar 
9b1(tha'o): khyim can/ gser mdog 'bar ba'i zhal mdog la/ gnam thags dbal gyi mche ba gcig pa/ dbu la stag gi thog zhu la/ mi 'di 'bar ba'i cod pan mnab pa/ lag na / 
9b2(tha'o): lthags kyi phur pa gu gang tsogs pa cig dang rtsi zhing rol pa las/ 'di dkar mda' gang tsam zhig thums su zhugs pa mas te/ nangs par nam langs rgungsad nas/ lus kyang yang / 
9b3(tha'o): ning lhums kyang 'jam snyams byed/ mdangs kyang za rgyas bzhin du gsal/ sems kyang nyi ma'i 'di ltar 'dzam/ stag za he tang rgyal mo ye/ yang rgyal ston la 'di skad zhus/ 
9b4(tha'o): yang rgyal lha ya rgyal po lags/ bdag ni za ma mo ye lus/ chags pa'i rang bzhin skyon che bas/ mdangs dang khar nub rmaMs lam na/ ya mtshan sprul pa'i cho 'drul gnyis/ 
9b5(tha'o): rnam du res bor zhugs pa rnaMs/ gcig ni rnam du gnod par zhugs/ gcigzhi rnam du phan par zhugs/ lha drin gang yin cha med kyi/ bon yul 'ol mo tshal yul gyi/ 
9b6(tha'o): mthing gur g.su 'theb gsas khang du/ bon sgom mdzad pa'i gnhen yod kyi/ yang rgyal lha yi rgyal po yi/ bon gyi sgom la zhus la spyod/ srid pa'i pa la dris la spyon/ mthing / 
10a1(tha'o): gur gsu 'thib gsas khang na/ can sgom mdzad pa'i gnhen la bhus/ 'gro ba'i don mdzad sprul pa'i gzhen/ stag za he ting rgyal mo yis/ mdang dang khar bub / 
10a2(tha'o): rmi lam du/ ya mtshan sprul pa'i cho 'dhrul gnyis/ rnam du res mos zhugs pa rmaMs/ lha srin gang yin cha med na/ srid pa'i gnhen la zhu ru mchis/ thugs kyi dgongs pas / 
10a3(tha'o): bshad du gsol/ zhes zhus pas/ pa yi bka' dang bon gyi gto/ ghen rab lha yi zhal nas r/ yang rgyal lha ye khab bdag pa/ stag za hi teng rgyal mo si/ sngon gyi las 
10a4(tha'o): 'phro dbang btsan te/ rgyu mthun bag chags rnam smin gyis/ srin gyi sprul pa gdong la zhugs/ srin la skyon che zhe sdug med/ rnam du ma la za zning skyes nas pa la zad
10a5(tha'o): sems can kun la gnod cing 'tshe bar byed/ rnam du gnod pa srin gyi bu yin te/ dge bcu gzhung du spyod pa dbyings kyi lha rnams thugs rjes gzigs/ g.sung drung lha yi sprul pa 
10a6(tha'o): ru/ mkha' 'gying gnhen rab sprul pa'i gsas/ lha yi sprul pa phyi nas zhugs/ srin po 'dul ba'i stobs dang ldan/ rnam la phan pa lha yi bu yin te/ yang rgyal lha yi sras po 
10b1(tha'o): / stag za he tang rgyal mo la/ lha dang rin gnyis skyes pa/ skyes pa'i che na ma brtag n/ lha rin bu gnyis mi shes pas/ pa dang bon dgri r myed/ zhes lung bstan no/ de / 
10b2(tha'o): nas yang rgyal lha yi rgyal po khab du sur log te/ las dge ba la yid gzhung ngo // gab pa gsang ba'i 'khor lo las/ sngon gyi las kyi rnam smin dang / sprul pa ci ltar byungs 
10b3(tha'o): ba'i mod 'grel lo// lha bu srin bu gnyis po de/ stag zar lhums su zhugs pa ni/ 'odi dkar thabs te pa yi rgyu/ 'di dmar shes rab yum gyi rgyu/ 'byung ba bzhi bskyed rtsa ru 
10b4(tha'o): 'brel/ bur ur po dang mer mer po/ gor gor po yai rang bzhin las/ lhe za lte 'khor chags pa'i rtsa/ btsug pa'i rtsa yi rtsa gnyis dkar dmar sbrel/ de la 'od zer nyi zla'i / 
10b5(tha'o): tshul/ bzhi skyes rtsa yi yan lag bzhi/ srog 'dzin ye shes 'brel rtsa lnga/ stobs kyi 'brel ba nyi hu byung / gab rtsa sum cu rtsa gnyis la/ 'brel rtsa sum cu rtsa gnyis / 
10b6(tha'o): byung / rtsa phran nyi khri gcig stong rgyas/ bye brag rtsa ya pa ma ni/ gu gu bzhin du bskres nas gnas/ yan lag mg dang dbang po chags/ ha khrag rus dang pags par 'brel/ 
11a1(tha'o): // 'jigs pa'i sgo lnga skar khung lnga/ brten pa'i gnas lngas rgyu yang bskyed/ 'khras pa'i mkhar lngas srog kyang bzung / srid pa'i chu bzhi dbugs kyang 'byin/ ril pa'i 
11a2(tha'o): mtsho bzhi mdangs kyang pbyung / gcod pa'i yul lnga longs spyod bskul/ rgyu ba'i srang gnyis lus zungs brnyan/ thabs kyi dum bur sa bon byas/ shes rab dum bur lus s+dzogs bskyed/ 
11a3(tha'o): srin ni rnam gyi g.yon du chags/ lha ni ru gyi g.yas su chags/ srin bu chags pa'i rnam skyin du/ na zhing tsha la slub cing le/ lha bu chags pa'i rnam g.yas ni/ bde zhing / 
11a4(tha'o): yang la 'jam zhing skyed/ lha yi thugs rje ma la byams/ srin gyi gdug tsub ma la sdang / de ltar chags shing sred pa'o// gab pa gsang ba'i 'khor lo las/ lha bu srin bu gnyis 
11a5(tha'o): yum gyi rnam du ji ltar chags pa bstan pa'i mod 'grel lo// de nas stag lo' lo 'gos la/ bco lnga rgung ginam langs kar/ rgyal po yab sum sras blhams pa/ lha bu 
11a6(tha'o): srin bu mtshe mar skyes/ sras cig sha mdangas dmar ba zhig/ sras cig zha mdangs dkar ba zhig/ lha srin gang yin cha med na/ yang rgyal lha yi rgyal po yi/ bon yul 'di ma 
11b1(tha'o): tshal yul gyi/ mthing gur g.su 'thib gsas khang na/ dgongs pa mdzad pa'i gshen la zhus/ gshen rab bla ma thugs rje'i mgon/ stag za he ting rgyal mo la/ lha srin bu / 
11b2(tha'o): gnyis mtsho bar skyes/ cig ni nha mdog dmar bzhig/ cigzhi na mdangs dkar b cig/ lha ren gang yin cha ma byed/ bdag cag mig tog pa can/ shes rab y shes 
11b3(tha'o): spyan dang ldan/ lha yi bka' stsol lung nod la/ pa la rthad cing bon la thu/ de skad ces zhus pas/ gnhen rab lha yis bka' bsrtsal pa/ stag za hi tang rgyal mo la/ lha 
11b4(tha'o): srin bu gnyis skyes pa ni/ gcig ni bar tshod bdud kyi bu/ gcig ni smon lam lha yi bu/ rgyu rkyen nyis mig ngas bshad kyis/ lus thud dbang po brtyan par nyon/ khyed cag rgyal po 
11b5(tha'o): stang dbyal gnyis/ sngon cho skye bsnga ma la/ 'di ma mdzes pa'i tshal glang du/ rgyal po gsr 'di 'bar ba dang / rgyal mo legs pa'i rgyal shron gnyis/ 'khor g.sog bran 
11b6(tha'o): 'khor mang pos bskor/ longs spyod bde zhing 'tshogs pa'i che/ bran ma d gong de dang 'thab/ bran gyi dzo mo yum la ldog/ rdo mos rgyal po yab la bskul/ yab kyis sum gyi 
12a1(tha'o): / by/ kha bzung ste/ thags kyi thu lum 'bar ba cig/ phyag gis brim pas bran phug bsad// de tshe rgyal po stang dbyal gnyis/ shin tu 'gyod cing thugs skyengs nas/ yi mug / 
12a2(tha'o): g chad sgyre ngag 'don/ dad pa'i rlan la snying rje' ser/ dge ba'i stobs bskyed smon lam btab/ sbyin pa dmigs pa med par btang / tshogs kyi 'khor lo grangs med bskor/ rin 
12a3(tha'o): chen sna tshogs mchod pa phrul/ bka' yi 'khor lo yongs su bskor/ smon lam dus dang grangs med btab/ skye ba de la tshe 'phos nas/ smon lam gcig tu btabs pa'i bthus/ 
12a4(tha'o): 'dod spyod 'tshogs pa lha yai gnas/ srid yul lha mdangs gnas su skye/ yi srid pbya yis bskos btab nas/ sngon gyi rgyal po yab sum gnyis/ yang rgyal lha yi rgyal po dang / 
12a5(tha'o): stag za he ting sras su 'khrungs/ sngon gyi bran dug bsad pa ni/ sngon gyi ba yum gyi ltor zhugs/ ma skyes rnam du zhugs tsam nas/ ma la mtha' mnar lan chags skyes/ 
12a6(tha'o): skyes nas lus s+dzogs zhed ldan nas/ pha la srog gi lan chags gnyer/ de nas sems can kun la gnod// sngon gyi smon lam dge stobs kyis/ lha dang gnhen gyi thugs rje ru/ 
12b1(tha'o): 'dul ba'i gnyen por sprul pa btang / de yang rgyal po chen po 'di lta ste/ sngon gyi dad pa'i rlan la snying rje'i ser bslang nas/ dge ba'i stobs bskyed pa ni/ da lha 'dod spyod tshangs pa lha 
12b2(tha'o): yi gnas su skyes pa lags so// smon lam grangs med gcig tu btab pa'i mthus/ da lha yang rgyal po yab yum stang dbyal zhal 'tshoMs pa lags so// bka'i 'khor lo / 
12b3(tha'o): bskor ba'i byin rlabs kyis/ da yang gnhen rabng yi zhal mthong lung znod pa lags so// tshogs kyi 'khor lo brgya rtsa brgyad bskor ba'i byin brlabs kyis/ dbang gi lha mkha' 
12b4(tha'o): 'gying kha yis/ srin po 'dul ba'i gnyen por btang ba lags so// sbyin pa dmigs pa med par btang pa'i byin brlabs kyis/ da lha yang 'dod spyod tshangs pa lha yi gnas na/ ma 
12b5(tha'o): 'dzad pa'i gter la longs spyod pa lagsso// yang rgyal lha ya rgyal po lags/ lha bsrin bu cha med na/ sha mdangs dkar ba lha lags kyis/ lha la stag gini lud dang / sa 
12b6(tha'o): mdangs dmar bsrin lags kyis/ de la sha dang khrag lud dang / dkar gsum gsol ba lha yi sras/ dmar gsum za ba srin gyi bu/ lha srin bu gnyis de ltar lags/ da yang rgyal / 
13a1(tha'o): pe yab sum gnyis/ las dang dge ba'i stobs bskyed d// snying rje bsam dang ldan par gyis/ zhes gshen rab kyis lung bstan pas/ rgyal po nyid kyang che snga bye dang / las / 
13a2(tha'o): rgyu 'bras dran par gyur te/ shin tu 'gyod sems drag po skyes nas/ slar khab tu byin/ yum la ston pa'i bka' lung bzhin du bstan nas/ dad pa dang don stobs bskyed/ bsam pa 
13a3(tha'o): dang snying rje'i ngang la gnas par bya'o// gab pa gsang ba'i 'khor lo las yum la sras bltams pa dang / skye gnas sprul pa bstan pa'i mdo 'grel lo// de nas rgyal po stang dbyal 
13a4(tha'o): gyis/ sha mdangas dkar ba'i sras po la/ stag mo grus ma'i zho bzhis te/ sras la rkan phab stag zhos gsoMs/ zhal zas dkar gsum gsol ba la/ sha mdangas dmar ba'i sras 
13a5(tha'o): po la/ phag chen smos pa'i khrag byud pas/ srin gyi ha khrag rus la 'cha'/ dmar gsum zas su zos pa la/ zhal zas gzhan la za ma 'dod/ rgyal bu de nyid tshang nas tshang 
13a6(tha'o): tshar du / lha yi bu ni stag zhes gsoMs/ srin gyi bu ni sha dang khrag gis gsos/ stag zhes gseMs pa'i lha bu ni/ pa la byams shing ma la gdung / sems can kun la brtse 
13b1(tha'o): sems che/ g.yung dung bon gyi rjes su 'dzug/ mtshan yang rgyal bu stag skyes lha yi bu zhes bya bar btags/ khrag gis gses pa'i srin bu ni/ pha la 'tshig cing ma la sdang //

21b4(tha'o): rgyud bskul gyi dbang dang rtsa gsum/ brnag pa las kyi dbang dang rtsa bzhi/ yongs s+dzogs gtor ma'i dbang dang rtsa lnga bskur ro// de yang ka ba nag po'i sgrub thabs su/ s+dzogs pa rnam 
21b5(tha'o): lnga bka' stsal/ ra rang nag po'i sgrub thabs su/ khug ma rnam pa lnga bka' stsal/ sha 'bal nag po'i sgrub thabs su/ gsang ba nag po'i rgyud gsum bka' stsal/ de ltar 
21b6(tha'o): srid pa'i rtse mor/ phyi dbang bskur zhing sgrub lung bstan pa'i mdo 'grel lo// de nas nang dbang bskur ba'i phyir/ gnhen rab lha yi dgongs pa yi/ dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor spyan drangs 
22a1(tha'o): te/ mchod cing bstyod dang bshags prul nas/ ting 'dzin dkyil 'khor gnas su bstam/ las kyi sems dpar dbang bskur nas/ byin rlabs bsnyen pa rdzogs par byas/ 
22a2(tha'o): de nas 'jug pa'i rim pa ni/ yang gsang lha yi rgon dug skor/ sgrol byed tom khung dmar nag tu/ byin rlabs dbang la gagsel yis/ log lha dam sri po mo sgrol/ las kyi 
22a3(tha'o): bum par bgegs rnams bkrad/ khro ba bcu yi mnan gzer bri/ 'chug dbang med par gnan te bzhag/ yum chen lnga yi nan gyis gsor/ thi sta ral gris phyag rgyas bcad/ 
22a4(tha'o): lha yi dgon phug bar gsum du / yid 'ong mdzes pa'i ma 'dal rtsar/ dag pa khus kyi bum pa yis/ phyi rabs gsang ba'i khrus rnams bya/ byang chub mchog tu mos sems bskyed/ 
22a5(tha'o): sngags dang dam tshig gsang sdom bshad/ dam chu bdud rtsi le la bnag/ skal ldan dad mos lha yi sras/ de rang pan chad rigs kyi bu/ khyod kyi srung ba'i dam tshig ni/ lha dang slob 
22a6(tha'o): dpon g.yung drung mched/ skad cig tsam yang yang mi rung / sngags dang dam tshig rgyun mi bcad/ sngags pas man ngag gnyer gtad pas/ gzhan la bstan cing bsgrag pa men/ 'di / 
22b1(tha'o): nas sku gsung thugs kyi las/ rtsa ba'i dam tshig gnyen po ste/ gal te 'di nas 'das sam na/ bskal pa gsum du 'khor bar ltung / mi bde sdug bsngal nyams su myong / bded /

22b6(tha'o): gsal bar dmigs phyes dkyil 'khor bstan/ stag skyes bu yis me tog gtor/ gang la bab pa rigs kyi lha/ dbang gi lha ru mkha' 'gying thob/ gtso ba'i mchog tu de bsgom / 
23a1(tha'o): pas/ mtshog dang thun mong dngos grub tob/ dereng pan chad bu khyod kyisg/ stag skyes lta bu'i mngkhor nas/ lha dang gzhen gyi gsang mtshan du/ rtag la mi 'bar dbal / 
23a2(tha'o): gyi sras/ lha sras gnhen gyi gdug oba tu/ sku gsung thugs kyi brda' rtags su/ bso A za la he du/ re re re r/ zhes pas/ gsang mtshan ming dbang bskur ro// de nas dbang bskur 
23a3(tha'o): te/ dbu rgyan blangs la/ o bon dbyings nam mkha'i nag tshul las/ skye med ng la s+dzogs pa'i sku/ ma pang gnhen lha khri khug dang / y srid mkha' 'gying rnam pa lnga/ rgyan dang yo 
23a4(tha'o): byad phun sum 'tshogs/ yid bzhin nor bu rin po che/ thugs rje dpag tu med pa yi/ rigs lnga lha yi pho brang 'dir/ dbus kyi gnas lngar dbang bskur ro// a o~M hUM shA/ 
23a5(tha'o): ces pas/ rigs lnga'i dbang bskur ro// de nas bum pa blangs la/ bum pa lha ya gzhal yas khang / sa bon yig 'bru'i 'phro 'du las/ dkyil 'khor lha dang so so' sku/ ma rig 
23a6(tha'o): dug lnga 'dul ba'i phyir/ mkha' 'gying rig pa'i ye shes lha/ sku la khra gsas khyung rgod de/ gsung la dbal gsas me 'bar nyid/ thugs la 'brug gss chem pa'i gtso/ yin / 
23b1(tha'o): tan me gsas kham nag 'bar/ phrin las klog gsas 'di 'gyu grub/ log 'dren regs pa 'dul ba'i phyir/ dug lnga khris pa'i khro bo lnga/ las dang bag chags 'dul ba'i phyir/ 
23b2(tha'o): shes rab dbyings la ysum bcu srul/ skyon gyi bar chod sel ba'i phyir/ sgo ba yab yum sprul pa'i lha/ bum pa lha yi so brang 'dis/ byin rlabs dbang bskur rgyas gdab pas/ 
23b3(tha'o): stag gsas khro bar dbang thob shig/ e kha ta tsha ba he bu/ ces khro ba yab yum rtsa ba'i lha rnams kyi dbang bskur ro// de nas yum bskyed la/ shes rab dbyings kyi rang bzhin 
23b4(tha'o): las/ thugs rje byams ma sprul pa'i yum/ khros pa'i tshul du stong khyab ma/ sras mo lnga dang sprul pa'i tshogs/ brtsi gdung yum du dbang bskur bas/ bde gnas gsang dbang thob 
23b5(tha'o): par shig/ me mu buM/ zhes pas brtse gdung yum gyi dbang bskur ro// de nas nyungs kar blangs la/ thabs dang shes rab 'gug sgrol las/ khra thabs gze ma 'gug sgrol tshogs/ 
23b6(tha'o): khra gsas khyung sman 'du 'phro ru/ khra spyang mgyogs ma pho nya'i tshogs/ yid sems sprul pa'i sbyor ba yi/ sems kyi ma mo khro chung tshogs/ pho nya sprul par dbang bskur bas// 
24a1(tha'o): gnas nas bsgral ba'i dbang thob zhig/ ei he ra ra ra khug khug/ zhes pas 'gug byed po nya'i dbang bskur ro// de nas ral gri blangs la/ gzi brjod dbang g.sul / 
24a2(tha'o): pa las/ 'jig rten las kyi dreg pa mo// ltham dral brgya dang rtsa brgyad kyis/ sgrol ba'i gang du dbang bskur bas/ log 'dran srin po sgrol bar zhog/ tab ta khyi la ha tu nan/ 
24a3(tha'o): ma ra ya cad/ zhes pas sgrol byed las mkhan gyi dbang bskur ro// de nas thun por blangs la/ 'jigs byed lha yinga rgyal du / spyi gtsug mgrin pa snying kha dang / lte ba gsang

24a5(tha'o): ye dza la par se/ zhes pas ngan sngags 'khor lo'i dbang bskur ro// m shig phyag rgya' dbang bskur bas/ gzugs pung rtog pa'i rgyud grol nas/ brjid 'gying sku yi dbang thob zhog/ 
24a6(tha'o): oM snying po sngags kyi dbang bskur bas/ ngag gi nyes pa'i skyon grol nas/ tsham sngam gsung dang ldan gyur cig/ a ting 'dzin dgongs pas dbang bskur bas/ rnam rtog blo ya sgrib sbyang 
24b1(tha'o): nas/ s+dzu 'brul thugs kyi dbang thob shig/ hUM cod paN dar gyi dbang bskur bas/ mi nub bdud las rgyal ba dang / srid gsum zil gnon dbang thob shig/ he stag chas na bza'i 
24b2(tha'o): dbang bskur bas/ log 'dren bgegs las dpa' ba dang / bkrag gsal 'od zer dbang thob shog/ re phyag mtshan pur pas dbang bskur bas/ srid gsum 'byung po 'dul ba dang /

24b5(tha'o): dbyangs kyi dbang thob shog/ oM/ zhes nang dbang s+dzogs par dbang bskur ro// me re 'bar ba'i sgrub thabs su/ mtshong rnam pa lnga bka' bsrtsal/ yan lag gi rgyud bzhi' bsgrub 
24b6(tha'o): thabs su/ sgrub chung nyi shu rtsa gcig bka' stsal/ mkha' 'gying khro ba sku yi gnas drug nas/ drag sngags gdug pa'i 'khor lo drug byung ste/ spyi bo bde chen gyi 'khor lo / 
25a1(tha'o): nas/ mgo 'khor gyos su gzug pa'i drag sngags byung / bkgren pa longs spyod gsung gi 'khor lo las/ sar gyi rgyun gs bcad pa'i rag sngags byung / thags ba / 
25a2(tha'o): s+dzu 'phul bon gyi 'khor lo las/ bsgo 'big dran pa 'phrog pa'i drag sngags byung / lce ba sprul pa dbang bsgyur gyi 'khor lo las/ srid pa rtsad nas gcod pa'i drag sngags byung /

25a5(tha'o): las/ nang dbang bskur zhing lung nes par bstan pa'i mod 'grel lo// de nas gsang dbang bskur ba'i phyir/ dbal bon stag la me 'bar gyis/ lnga pung 'du ba'i phung po las/ lha yi / 
25a6(tha'o): dkyil 'khor bzhi ru byas/ 'byung ba nam mkha'i 'khor lo yis/ rnam shes dbugs bskyed zhe sdang thul/ 'byung ba sa yi 'khor lo yis/ tshor ba khrag bskyed 'dod chags thul// 
25b1(tha'o): 'byung bzlung gi 'khor lo las/ 'du byed dbugs bskyed 'phrag dog thul/ sku lus 'dam gang gru bzhi las/ dkyil 'khor byi y khyen dang sbyar/ srog dang gzung pa'i rtsa gnyis ni/ 
25b2(tha'o): tshangs pa'i thig gnyis dag dang sbyar/ gyes pa gab pa'i rtsa ba bzhi ni/ 'grus cig chen po bzhe dang sbyar/ gab rtsa sum chu rtsa gnyis ni/ gshag cig sum hu rtsa gnyis sbyar/

25b4(tha'o): thig bzhi dang sbyar bar bya/ bla rtsa skor thig gnyis dang sbyar/ ye shes rig pa'i rtsa lnga ni/ zlum cig lnga skor zla gam dang sbyar/ rtsa dang 'khor lo gnyis med 'brel/ bde chen 'khor 
25b5(tha'o): lo 'di 'pro'i gnas/ longs spyod 'khor lo bye brag 'byed/ bon gyi 'khor lo 'byed pa'i gni/ nang gi 'di lnga lha ya gnas/ rhe mtshong gyur smrag po na/ gtso ba lha sa gnal / 
25b6(tha'o): yas bskyed/ shel gyi kha bad dkar po ni/ steng phyogs khro ba'i gzhal yas khang / rtse mo thig le 'dus pa'i gdan/ 'og phyogs khro ba'i gzhal yas khang / glo ba'i 'khor lo / 
26a1(tha'o): // rtsibs brgyad ni/ phyogs mtshams khro ba'i gzhal yas khang / leb rgan yol bas bcad pa ni/ me ro'i ra bas mngon rtogs rgyan/ mtchen pa khrag gi rgya mtsho /

26b5(tha'o): dbang dang / mi shig g.yung drung gi dbang dang / mnyam nyid ye s+dzogs dbang rnams bskur/ sku rnam pa lnga yis rgyas gdab/ ye shes lnga yi byin gyis brlabs/ de bas yang yang dbang re re / 
26b6(tha'o): la/ byin rlabs rang grol man ngag ri re bstan pa ni/ rig pa pyi brug gi man ngag dang / ye shes rang gsal gyi man ngag dang / bde ba dngos med kyi man ngag dang / snang ba rgyas 'deabs

28a1(tha'o): zhing gas ng ba'i gnyeir gtad pa/ don med gnan las la nhi snton me bya/ thags kyi dbm chig nyams nas dmyal ba'i rgyu/ bskal pa chen po gsum du thar mi /

28b6(tha'o): dam tshig nyi shu bstan/ khyad par lha gnas dam tshig ni/ mdo bsdus rtsa ba bzhi ru bstan/ spyod pa rgyun dang rang bzhin blta ba dang / lta ba'i nyams drid gal mdo nges dang bzhi/ de /

63b4(tha'o): len gzhi dken pas gam cha gsad du yin pa dang / sghes su de zhus bgrigs pa che yang mkhyen dpyed dab 'byams pa min chad/ 'di' thad mthun rkyen zung la 'gal rkyen myang ba'i gseb ru dal brling 'grig pa dang / 
63b5(tha'o): ma byung na/ phyegs gang so'i thad ypug dang gnas sdangs tsha las brsal ba'i legs ma zhig then thabs med pas/ de lugs kyis rjes su gzigs mtshan rnam pas 'di la dg rkyen thad ye bsrang yong nges gnang do me / 
63b6(tha'o): zhing / 'di yi byas pa 'dis kyang sad du g.yung dung ben gyi lung gi bstan pa don po che gsal dag 'grig po'i zhabs zhu' grabs bsdegs tsam du 'gyur rnyam che ba bcas/ 'byung ldan bdaba byung shing /
